lang="en">List of explorers</h1> <div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">\n<div class="noprint" id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div> <div id="contentSub"><div 2019</i>.</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<div id="jump-to-nav"></div> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>\n<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#p-search">Jump to search</a>\n<div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en"><div class="mw-parser-output"><p>\nThe following is a <b>list of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Explorer" title="Explorer">explorers</a></b>. Their common names, countries of origin (modern and former), centuries when they were active and main areas of exploration are listed below.\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:The_landing_of_Vikings_on_America.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2832" data-file-width="2159" decoding="async" height="197" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c0/The_landing_of_Vikings_on_America.jpg/150px-The_landing_of_Vikings_on_America.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c0/The_landing_of_Vikings_on_America.jpg/225px-The_landing_of_Vikings_on_America.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c0/The_landing_of_Vikings_on_America.jpg/300px-The_landing_of_Vikings_on_America.jpg 2x" width="150"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:The_landing_of_Vikings_on_America.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Leif_Erikson" title="Leif Erikson">Leif Erikson</a> was a famous Norse explorer who is credited for being the first European to set foot on <a href="/wiki/Americas" title="Americas">American</a> soil (c. 1000).</div></div></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Marco_Polo_Mosaic_from_Palazzo_Tursi.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1286" data-file-width="1024" decoding="async" height="188" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Marco_Polo_Mosaic_from_Palazzo_Tursi.jpg/150px-Marco_Polo_Mosaic_from_Palazzo_Tursi.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Marco_Polo_Mosaic_from_Palazzo_Tursi.jpg/225px-Marco_Polo_Mosaic_from_Palazzo_Tursi.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b0/Marco_Polo_Mosaic_from_Palazzo_Tursi.jpg/300px-Marco_Polo_Mosaic_from_Palazzo_Tursi.jpg 2x" width="150"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Marco_Polo_Mosaic_from_Palazzo_Tursi.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Marco_Polo" title="Marco Polo">Marco Polo</a> was an Italian explorer who traveled to the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Far_east" title="Far east">far east</a> and back to his hometown <a href="/wiki/Venice" title="Venice">Venice</a> in the matter of 24 years. He is noted for making detailed chronicles of his travels (1271-1295).</div></div></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Zhen_he.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1024" data-file-width="683" decoding="async" height="225" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cb/Zhen_he.jpg/150px-Zhen_he.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cb/Zhen_he.jpg/225px-Zhen_he.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cb/Zhen_he.jpg/300px-Zhen_he.jpg 2x" width="150"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Zhen_he.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Zheng_He" title="Zheng He">Zheng He</a> was a Chinese explorer who sailed along the Southeast Asian, South Asian, Western Asian, and East African coasts along with his fleet of incredibly large ships and several hundred men (1405-1433).</div></div></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Diogo_C%C3%A3o.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="220" data-file-width="150" decoding="async" height="220" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/c/cd/Diogo_C%C3%A3o.jpg" width="150"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Diogo_C%C3%A3o.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Portugal" title="Portugal"><img alt="Portugal" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="750" data-file-width="750" decoding="async" C&#227;o</a> is the first European to explore the <a href="/wiki/Congo_River" title="Congo River">Congo River</a> and the west coast of Africa, south of the <a href="/wiki/Equator" title="Equator">equator</a> (1482-1486).</div></div></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><a class="image" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/35px-Flag_of_England.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/46px-Flag_of_England.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> English <a href="/wiki/Privateer" title="Privateer">privateer</a> <a href="/wiki/Francis_Drake" title="Francis Drake">Francis Drake</a> plundered many Spanish towns and ships in the <a href="/wiki/Caribbean" title="Caribbean">Caribbean</a> and elsewhere. However, he is most notable for completing the second circumnavigation of the world (1577-1580).</div></div></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Samuel-de-champlain-s.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="590" data-file-width="454" decoding="async" height="195" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Samuel-de-champlain-s.jpg/150px-Samuel-de-champlain-s.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Samuel-de-champlain-s.jpg/225px-Samuel-de-champlain-s.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Samuel-de-champlain-s.jpg/300px-Samuel-de-champlain-s.jpg 2x" width="150"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Samuel-de-champlain-s.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_France" title="Kingdom of France"><img alt="Kingdom of France" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="800" data-file-width="1200" decoding="async" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9a/Royal_Standard_of_the_King_of_France.svg/23px-Royal_Standard_of_the_King_of_France.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9a/Royal_Standard_of_the_King_of_France.svg/35px-Royal_Standard_of_the_King_of_France.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9a/Royal_Standard_of_the_King_of_France.svg/45px-Royal_Standard_of_the_King_of_France.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Samuel_de_Champlain" title="Samuel de Champlain">Samuel de Champlain</a> is known as "The Father of <a href="/wiki/New_France" title="New France">New France</a>". He founded the first permanent European settlements in <a href="/wiki/Canada_(New_France)" title="Canada (New France)">Canada</a>, and explored many <a href="/wiki/Great_Lakes" title="Great Lakes">lakes</a> and rivers in the interior lands from early age to his death (1603-1635).</div></div></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:HenryHudson.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1065" data-file-width="987" decoding="async" height="162" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d2/HenryHudson.jpg/150px-HenryHudson.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d2/HenryHudson.jpg/225px-HenryHudson.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d2/HenryHudson.jpg/300px-HenryHudson.jpg 2x" width="150"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:HenryHudson.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Dutch_Republic" title="Dutch Republic"><img alt="Dutch Republic" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="300" data-file-width="450" decoding="async" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5d/Statenvlag.svg/23px-Statenvlag.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5d/Statenvlag.svg/35px-Statenvlag.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5d/Statenvlag.svg/45px-Statenvlag.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/England" title="England"><img alt="England" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="480" data-file-width="800" decoding="async" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/23px-Flag_of_England.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/35px-Flag_of_England.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/b/be/Flag_of_England.svg/46px-Flag_of_England.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> English explorer <a href="/wiki/Henry_Hudson" title="Henry Hudson">Henry Hudson</a> explored what is now <a href="/wiki/New_York_(state)" title="New York (state)">New York</a> and northeastern <a href="/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canada</a>. Today he has both a <a href="/wiki/Hudson_River" title="Hudson River">river</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hudson_Bay" title="Hudson Bay">bay</a> named after him  (1609-1611).</div></div></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Abeltasman1903.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="328" data-file-width="281" <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Abeltasman1903.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Dutch_Republic" title="Dutch Republic"><img alt="Dutch Republic" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="300" data-file-width="450" decoding="async" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5d/Statenvlag.svg/23px-Statenvlag.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5d/Statenvlag.svg/35px-Statenvlag.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5d/Statenvlag.svg/45px-Statenvlag.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Abel_Tasman" title="Abel Tasman">Abel Tasman</a> is the first known European to sight the islands of <a href="/wiki/Tasmania" title="Tasmania">Tasmania</a>, <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand" title="New Zealand">New Zealand</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Fiji" title="Fiji">Fiji</a> (1642-1643).</div></div></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Captainjamescookportrait.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1280" data-file-width="1020" decoding="async" height="188" class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Captainjamescookportrait.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Great_Britain" title="Kingdom of Great Britain"><img alt="Kingdom of Great Britain" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="1000" decoding="async" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Flag_of_Great_Britain_%281707%E2%80%931800%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_Great_Britain_%281707%E2%80%931800%29.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Flag_of_Great_Britain_%281707%E2%80%931800%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_Great_Britain_%281707%E2%80%931800%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Flag_of_Great_Britain_%281707%E2%80%931800%29.svg/46px-Flag_of_Great_Britain_%281707%E2%80%931800%29.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> <a href="/wiki/James_Cook" title="James Cook">James Cook</a>. Famous British explorer who led three voyages to the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pacific" title="Pacific">Pacific</a>. He is known for exploring and charting many islands in the ocean such as <a href="/wiki/Polynesia" title="Polynesia">Polynesia</a>, <a href="/wiki/New_Zealand" title="New Zealand">New Zealand</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Hawaiian_Islands" title="The Hawaiian Islands">The Hawaiian Islands</a>, and the eastern coast of <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a> (1768-1779).</div></div></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:152px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Nlc_amundsen.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="622" data-file-width="443" decoding="async" height="211" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7d/Nlc_amundsen.jpg/150px-Nlc_amundsen.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7d/Nlc_amundsen.jpg/225px-Nlc_amundsen.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7d/Nlc_amundsen.jpg/300px-Nlc_amundsen.jpg 2x" width="150"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Nlc_amundsen.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Norway" title="Norway"><img alt="Norway" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="800" data-file-width="1100" decoding="async" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d9/Flag_of_Norway.svg/21px-Flag_of_Norway.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d9/Flag_of_Norway.svg/32px-Flag_of_Norway.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d9/Flag_of_Norway.svg/41px-Flag_of_Norway.svg.png 2x" width="21"/></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Roald_Amundsen" title="Roald Amundsen">Roald Amundsen</a> was an explorer of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Polar_regions" title="Polar regions">polar regions</a>. He was the first person to reach the <a href="/wiki/South_Pole" title="South Pole">South Pole</a>, and eventually also reached the <a href="/wiki/North_Pole" title="North Pole">North Pole</a> by air (1910-1926).</div></div></div>\n<table class="wikitable sortable" style="text-align:center;">\n<tbody><tr>\n<th width="20%">Name\n</th>\n<th width="15%">Modern (and former) nationality\n</th>\n<th
